Over Eight Hundred Organizations and Two Hundred Thousand People 100

Hold Anti-Japanese National Salvation Assembly

Important Resolutions

Order the Japanese army to withdraw from occupied territories, or declare war. Support Commander-in-Chief Chiang's unified military power against Japan. Urge the Guangdong side to eliminate personal prejudices and unite against foreign enemies. Severely punish derelict officials such as Wang Zhengting and Zang Shiyi. Implement a conscription system with the goal of defeating Japan. Forever sever economic relations with Japan. Severely punish traitorous merchants.

The Citizens' Assembly of this city was held at the Public Sports Ground yesterday morning. All sectors of industry, commerce, and academia unanimously suspended business. The assembly ground was crowded with people, the atmosphere was solemn and stirring, and the anti-Japanese sentiment was exceptionally tense. The meeting adjourned at 12:15 PM. The details of the assembly are recorded as follows:

Organizations Present: City Party Headquarters · Various levels of Party Headquarters · Shanghai County Party Headquarters · Various District Farmers' Associations · Preparatory Committee of the City Education Association · Various District Education Associations · Great China University · Datong University · Jinan University · China Public Communications College · Fudan University · Law School · Chizhi College · School of Political Science and Law · Labor University · University of Shanghai · Central China Business College · Medical College · Tongji University · Shanghai High School · Jingye High School · Junyi High School · Nanshi and Beishi High Schools · etc., large and small schools · Postal Service · Publishing Industry · Cigarette Industry · Water and Electricity Industry · Pharmaceutical Industry · Knitting Industry · Cotton Textile Industry · Shipbuilding Industry, etc., over one hundred industries Anti-Japanese National Salvation Assembly of Shanghai City (Photo by this newspaper)

Assembly Order: (1) Everyone stands at attention, (2) Play mourning music, (3) Presidium takes their seats, (4) Sing the Party song, (5) Pay the highest respect to the Party and National flags and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, (6) Read Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will respectfully, (7) Observe three minutes of silence to mourn the compatriots in distress, (8) Chairman's report, (9) All executive committee members of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association take the oath of office, (10) Discussion of proposals, (11) Unscheduled motions, (12) Speeches from all sectors, (13) Shout slogans, (14) Parade, (15) Adjournment.

Chairman's Report: The Presidium nominated Wang Xiaolai to report, which roughly stated, "The fall of the Northeast has shocked the whole country. Our people regard this brutal Japan as a mortal enemy. This illegal occupation of our Northeast is in fact the result of their long-standing plan, and is the prelude to their destruction of our country. Everyone must know that if the three eastern provinces are lost, the future disasters for our country will be a hundred or a thousand times greater than today. Therefore, at this critical moment, at this time of national survival, our 400 million people should uphold the great principle of being responsible for survival and rise up together with the determination to 'wear our hair and tie our crowns', rather be cannon fodder than be subjugated slaves, and decide to wage war on the battlefield and commercial war in the marketplace to protect our territory and avenge our country, and vow to wipe out this great shame." (The following is omitted)

Committee Members' Oath: After the Chairman's report, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association committee members took the oath. The oath read, "We swear to accept the entrustment of the representatives of all groups in the city with the utmost sincerity, to uphold the spirit of the Three Principles of the People, to work hard for the anti-Japanese national salvation cause, and we will never be greedy for life or afraid of death, or engage in private gain or malpractice. If we dare to violate this oath, we are willing to accept the most severe punishment. We swear." The oath-takers were all executive committee members: Hou Dachun · Li Yongxiang · Lu Jingshi · Wang Wenhua · Wang Zhuping · Chen Peide · Tang Junsheng · Zhou Xuexiang · Wang Xiaolai · Zheng Chengqing · Wang Hanliang · Fang Jiaobo · Ye Huijun · Wang Yansong · Yu Qiaqing · Chen Songyuan · Yu Hualong · Zhang Yichen · Hu Fengxiang · Cheng Zhusun · Wang Jiean · Lu Xingzhuang · Liu Shimu · Zhang Honghai · Tao Baichuan · Tong Xingbai · Feng Yixian · Chen Yafu · Zhang Huijun · Lin Kecong · Wang Xiaoying · Chen Tingrui · Li Cishan · Yan Esheng · Zhu Yingpeng · Xi Yushu · Li Wenjie · Shi Liangcai · Wu Mai · Wang Boqi · Wu Zhihao · Zhao Jijin · Xu Wei · Zhu Xuefan · Lu Muqin · Wang Changyuan · Gu Ruofeng · Gong Yuting · Fu Dewei · Yu Zhongxian · Luo Qinghua · Ma Shaoquan · Zhang Zilian · Liu Jincao · Ren Jinpin · Liu Zhanen · Lin Kanghou · Chu Huiseng · Xie Fusheng · Dong Xianguang · Hu Shuhua · (Alternate Committee Members) Chen Haiqiu · Xu Jilou · Ye Jiaxing · Zhao Shusheng · Yu Zhenhui · Wang Yuxiang · Long Peiyun · Wang Pingnan · Xu Muo · Jin Chuxiang · Zhang Tianbai · Cao Zhigong · Qiu Zitong · Zheng Hairuo.

Resolutions Passed: After the committee members took the oath, the following proposals were unanimously agreed upon by the entire venue: (1) Telegraph the central government, ordering the Japanese troops and soldiers to withdraw from all occupied territories, (1) (3) Stores close (2) Students parade (4) Laborers love their country (Photo by this newspaper)

Otherwise, sever diplomatic relations with Japan and declare war; (2) Telegraph support for Commander-in-Chief Chiang to unify military power, concentrate military force, and prepare to confront Japan with strength; Assembly Declaration: This time, the Japanese imperialists, taking advantage of our country's time of natural disasters and bandit troubles, dared to defy the great injustice of the world, suddenly sent troops to the Northeast, forcibly occupied our country's territory, brutally murdered our officials and people, looted our property, burned our arsenal, occupied our armory, and destroyed our railways, blocking our transportation. When the bad news came, everyone was furious. All our people were filled with indignation and shared the same hatred for the enemy, vowing not to coexist under the same sky. More than eight hundred organizations and over two hundred thousand citizens in this city held a Citizens' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Assembly this morning, raising their arms and shouting, with ten thousand voices roaring, with grief and passion, which can be said to be unprecedented. Our countrymen are grieving over the country's current difficulties and lamenting the imminent destruction of the country. However, judging from the people's sentiments today, there is still hope, and the country's fate can be saved. If we act now, how can we fear the brutal Japan? Although the brutal Japan has not yet been punished by heaven, when our people unanimously reach the point of being unable to bear it, they will surely weep blood and sleep on their weapons, and fight a decisive battle with the brutal Japan, rather be shattered like jade than remain intact like tile. The 60 million people on the three islands can never be the enemy of our 400 million people. Life and death, survival and destruction, depend on how hard the people of our country struggle. Today's assembly resolutions are not only an essential plan to save the country from its current destruction, but also the entrustment of the ardent hopes of the people of the whole country. Fortune and misfortune, survival and destruction, depend on this one move. May our compatriots rise up and plan for it urgently. Our sincere words, we hope you will consider them carefully.

Crowd Parade: The parade route was predetermined by the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. It started from the Public Sports Ground, went along Fangxie Road to Laoximen, then along Zhonghua Road through Xiaodongmen, then along Minguo Road, circled the city for a week, and dispersed at Laobeimen. During the parade, all members of the Postal Workers' Union rode bicycles as a vanguard, followed by the Party Headquarters, then women, then students, workers, merchants, farmers, and finally the Boy Scouts. Along the way, they distributed anti-Japanese leaflets and shouted anti-Japanese slogans. The emotions were tense and the order was quite good.

Other Assembly News: After the adjournment at 12:45 PM this afternoon, over seven thousand people from six groups, including Jinan University, China Public School, Labor University, Cultural College, and the Eighth and Tenth Cotton Textile Industry Unions, were delayed because they were far away in Zhenru and Jiangwan and had inconvenient transportation. Seeing that the assembly had dispersed, they were very disappointed. At that time, the assembly chairmen Lu Jingshi, Hou Dachun, and Tao Baichuan were still at the venue taking care of the crowd, so Tao Baichuan, on behalf of the chairmen, reported on the proceedings and resolutions of the assembly. Telegram from the County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association 102

Telegraph urging Northeast generals to save the country with force

The Shanghai County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association yesterday sent a telegram to the Northeast generals, saying: "To the commanding officers of the Northeast armies, as reported by newspapers nationwide: The Japanese imperialists, taking advantage of our country's multiple disasters and frequent calamities, dare to defy the great injustice of the world, disrupt world peace, send troops to the three eastern provinces, forcibly occupy our Liaoyang, brutally murder our compatriots, burn our armories, and detain our officials. They are wild and barbaric, and have no regard for our country. Recently, they have dispatched a large number of gunboats to blockade the seaports, probe key passes, invade from the south and attack from the north, attempting to annex China once and for all. The life and death of our Chinese nation is at stake. All our people should risk their lives for the final struggle. If we still adopt a policy of non-resistance and dream of prolonging our lives, not only will the pain of national subjugation be immediately apparent, but this servile nation will be forever recorded in world history and will be laughed at by Korea and India. Gentlemen, you command hundreds of thousands of troops in the Northeast. The state raises soldiers to defend the country and protect the people. At this time of foreign humiliation and national crisis, it is the time for soldiers to use their weapons. The people pay taxes and levies to support the soldiers, and this is the time to receive the reward. As soldiers, even if they are crushed to pieces, they will not hesitate to fulfill their duty as soldiers and meet the ardent expectations of the people. Not only that, soldiers are also citizens. If the country is destroyed, the people will be slaves, so how can soldiers be safe in their positions? Moreover, most of you are from the Northeast. As Japanese soldiers run rampant, the bones of your ancestors are exposed, your families are either raped or kidnapped, your property has been reduced to nothing, and your homes have been turned into ruins. If the Xiongnu are not destroyed, how can we have a home? Therefore, even if you do not consider the country and the people, but for the sake of your own ancestors, you should rectify your troops, die on the battlefield, be loyal to the country, be filial to your ancestors, sacrifice yourself for righteousness, and give up your life for justice. In this way, your names will be immortal for thousands of years. Our compatriots across the country have worked together and taken a unified step, ready to fight to the death. We hope that you will resolutely use force to deal with them and save the nation from danger. China is fortunate, and the Chinese nation is fortunate. Shanghai County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee."

Letter requesting the Ministry of Industry and Commerce Inspection Bureau to issue a catalog of Japanese goods. The Shanghai County Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee yesterday sent a letter to the Industrial and Commercial Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, saying: "Regarding the fact that the brutal Japan is running rampant and we can no longer tolerate it, we have decided to sever economic relations with Japan and are actively implementing it. However, because there are so many types of Japanese goods sold in China, there are often omissions during inspection. We are afraid that shameless merchants will pass off inferior goods as good, or that inspection personnel will not be able to identify them, resulting in smuggling, which will have a huge impact on the anti-Japanese future. Therefore, we are specially writing to your bureau to quickly publish a catalog of Japanese goods and send several copies for reference and to facilitate inspection."

Their intention was very good.

Worker Li Jinshan Commits Suicide by Poisoning: Li Jinshan, a native of Anhui, lived at No. 159 Nanyao, near Shenyuan. He used to work as a foreman in the burlap factory of the Japanese company Dongya Co., Ltd. Yesterday, he went to the Public Sports Field to participate in the Citizens' Congress. After the congress was dismissed, he was stimulated and filled with indignation. He secretly went to a pharmacy to buy sleeping pills and swallowed them in secret, attempting to end his life. When he returned home, his family called him to eat, but Li remained silent, his face pale. After his wife repeatedly questioned him, he could no longer speak, only pointing to his mouth with his finger. He was immediately rushed to a nearby hospital for treatment. According to the doctor's examination, it seemed that he had swallowed corrosive sublimate and his life was in danger.

Important News from Anti-Japanese Circles in Aviation 106

Liaoning Refugees Arrive in Shanghai: Japanese troops suddenly forcibly occupied Liaoning on the 18th. On the 19th, Japanese troops went out to cause trouble in the city of Liaoning, forcibly entering shops and homes to rob and loot at will, and there were also cases of rape. The people of Liaoning fled in droves amidst the artillery fire. People from Zhili, Shandong and Henan all fled to Tianjin and Beijing, while people from the South fled south to Tianjin, and some fled to Dalian to come to Shanghai. Yesterday, the first batch of refugees arrived in Shanghai from Shenyang, having traveled by sea from Dalian to Shanghai, a total of one hundred and seventeen people. Because they were unable to carry their belongings when they escaped, most of them escaped with only the clothes on their backs. Therefore, they were in a very sorry state when they arrived in Shanghai. Among this batch of refugees were 51 men, including Zhou Hefu, Zhu Yunsheng, Chen Hanxian, Sun Jifang, and Lu Jianqing, and 66 women and children, all of whom lived in the city of Fengtian and Xiaonanguan. Among them, businessmen accounted for 70%, and the rest were teachers and other professions. According to a reporter speaking with a refugee, after the Japanese troops entered Shenyang, they fired guns and cannons indiscriminately at our soldiers and civilians. The number of people who died in the artillery fire was countless. The next day, they went out to arrest people. Those in Liaoning who had a slight reputation and advocated resistance against Japan were arrested and killed. Japanese soldiers freely entered people's homes and shops, searching for cash and violating women. The residents of the city were all in danger. The country has not yet been destroyed, but the people of Liaoning have suffered the slaughter of the violent Japanese. The residents of the Eastern Province have already experienced it, so they would rather abandon their property in Liaoning and flee with the clothes on their backs. When each person escaped from Liaoning, they were in great difficulty. Some of the people from the Southern provinces went to Tianjin and then to Shanghai, and some took the sea route from Dalian to Shanghai. When each person left Liaoning, they only brought a little money. Even if they had savings, they were in the bank, which was controlled by the Japanese, and they could not withdraw it. Therefore, they were in a very sorry state when they arrived in Shanghai, and they were in tears when they spoke. It was also said that the second batch of refugees from the Southern provinces would arrive in Shanghai soon. This time, the refugees who escaped were only a part of the people from the Southern provinces. The property they abandoned and lost amounted to millions, and the number of people who were brutally killed by the Japanese soldiers has not yet been ascertained. The Current Situation of Effective Resistance to Goods: Before the 18th of this time, although the anti-Japanese association strictly inspected, there were still some Japanese goods that were loaded privately, and goods from the East could not be completely stopped. Since the Japanese troops occupied Liaoning, the business circles in Shanghai have made major decisions to thoroughly reject Japanese goods. Since the 23rd, the Japanese Qing Yangtze River ships have not loaded any export goods, and the Japanese Post Office's Sino-Japanese liners have also not loaded any Chinese goods in recent days. The customs declaration agencies have agreed that all customs declaration personnel will not be allowed to go to Japanese shipping companies or other commercial banks from now on, so that trade between Japanese goods and the Chinese people can be fundamentally severed. In recent days, Japanese ships on all routes have been leaving empty. Recently, even the Yangtze River Japanese ships have no Chinese passengers.

Press Conference Reception

Correspondents from Various Countries Stationed in Shanghai 107

Hoping to Uphold Justice and Provide Accurate Reports

Japan Cannot Evade Blame for the Manchurian Incident

Since Japan used force to seize our Liaoning and Jilin provinces, people from various countries have been paying close attention to the Manchurian issue. Foreign-run newspapers and news agencies have been competing to publish news reports, which have a significant impact on foreign readers. Recognizing this, the Shanghai Journalists Association held a reception for foreign correspondents at the Cathay Hotel at 4:00 PM yesterday, aiming to enable figures in the press of friendly nations to understand the various atrocities committed by the Japanese in suddenly and violently seizing our territory, violating international law, and contravening the Anti-War Pact, as well as the attitudes held by the Chinese populace. More than fifty reporters and guests from various Western newspapers and news agencies attended. Yan Duhe, Zhu Yingpeng, and Hang Shijun were elected as the presidium. Details are as follows:

Attendees: The foreign newspaper and news agency reporters who attended were Remy, Kwongda (representing Agence France-Presse, Chinese National Magazine), Flandin (representing North-China Daily News), Isaacs (representing Shanghai Times), Prawdzic (representing Trans-Ocean News Agency), Miss Schmetzer (representing German newspaper Frankfurter Zeitung), Mairesse (representing French newspaper Le Journal de Shanghai), Snow (representing Millard's Review), Sweetland (representing Chicago Daily News), Meggyesy (representing United Press), Chancelor Cox (representing Reuters), Bob (representing Associated Press Association), Punhasda, and others. Other attendees included Zhang Zhuping, Dong Xian Guang, Wang Boqi, Wang Zhongwei, Nie Shifen, Mrs. Ma Jiashou, Yang Xiaotang, Xu Jianping, Wang Yingbin, Xie Fusheng, Wu Tingchen, Zhu Xinong, Sun Daosheng, Qian Hua, Zhou Fanping, Qian Bohan, Yu Kongwo, Jiang Jianhou, Jin Huating, Xu Chihen, Fan Jingwu, Tang Demin, and more than fifty others.

Chairman's Address: Chairman Yan Duhe delivered the opening address, which was translated into English by Wang Yingbin. The gist of his speech was to first state the purpose of the Shanghai Journalists Association's reception for foreign reporters. Amid feelings of gratitude, there was a sense of sorrow and indignation. Because Japan's military occupation of Liaoning and Jilin provinces was an unprecedented act of barbarism in the international community, the loss of life and property suffered by the Chinese people was incalculable, and the atrocities continue unabated. Secondly, he stated that although the Chinese government and people are extremely indignant at Japan's violence against China, they are mostly maintaining calm and patience, knowing that force will ultimately be defeated by justice and that international conventions will have the effect of curbing violence. The League of Nations and the United States have both issued telegrams to stop Japan's atrocities, and China is very grateful for these actions upholding justice. At this point, Yan called attention to how Japan has been confusing the public and distorting right and wrong. He said that Japan's actions, which disregard justice and violate conventions, are by no means just an issue confined to parts of Liaoning and Jilin, but a significant issue affecting world peace. Finally, Yan forcefully stated that in addition to relying on its military violence, Japan is also using deceptive tactics to vigorously promote its false propaganda, hoping that the gentlemen of the press from friendly nations present would uphold justice and provide accurate reports, so that people of friendly nations can learn about China's true attitude and expose Japan's cunning and deceitful methods of fabrication.

Dong's Speech: Dong's speech mainly stated that today, the Shanghai Journalists Association is hosting this event for the Japanese occupation of Manchuria, and he had been invited to attend and offer his humble opinions. Regarding the various circumstances of the Manchurian issue, he had repeatedly written about them in the Continental Times, so there was no need to repeat them. Now, he would offer a few observations as follows: The Shanghai Journalists Association, composed of reporters from various Chinese-language daily newspapers in Shanghai, has considerable influence. Today's gathering with everyone is to express the association's views to everyone present. At this point, Dong recounted the origins of the Incident in the Three Northeastern Provinces and the seriousness of the situation, and then said that the pen of a journalist should fight for justice, and he believed that fellow journalists around the world would also express their fair opinions. Dong continued that the current Japanese atrocities in Liaodong are not just a local dispute between China and Japan, but an obstacle to world peace, and he hoped that everyone present would pay attention to this point. Dong also elaborated on how the Manchurian issue could affect the world situation, moving everyone who listened, and said that he could not help but feel disappointed upon hearing the news that the League of Nations was not involved in this matter, but still could not say that there was no hope, because if others cannot help us, we must help ourselves. Manchuria is an important territory of China, rich in resources, and sufficient to solve China's problem of overpopulation. As for the Japanese, they also want to seize South Manchuria due to their own domestic overpopulation, but the result will not only fail to solve the difficulties of the population problem, but will instead cause disputes and endanger the world situation. What will be the ultimate gains and losses? Finally, Dong said that the purpose of today's tea party is to request the foreign reporters present to adopt a fair attitude and announce the truth of the Manchurian issue to people in Europe and America, so that the rights and wrongs of this matter can receive a fair judgment, saying, "The pen is mightier than the sword," and hoped that colleagues around the world would not be subdued by military force, as the League of Nations' attitude is today.

Zhou's Speech: Zhou Fanping, a reporter from the North-China Daily News, said in his speech that he was not speaking in the capacity of a journalist, nor was he giving a propaganda-style speech, but only expressing his personal opinion from the standpoint of the Chinese people. Today, China is in a difficult situation, and what can save it is only the spirit of the new China. What Chinese history shows us is only that we have been invaded by others and have never inflicted violence on others. This is not cowardice, but because China has always been known to the world for its peace and patience. The Manchurian Incident is something that no one can tolerate. At present, China does not seek the favor of others, but only justice. He earnestly hoped that the foreign reporters present would use fair eyes to judge this incident.

Speeches by Foreign Guests: Foreign reporters and guests who spoke included Remy, Meggyesy, and Nie Ganfen. Remy was the first to stand up and address the audience when the chairman asked the Western reporters to express their views. He said that he had been engaged in journalism in China for more than fifty years and was quite familiar with the situation in China. He expressed his sympathy for the attitude of the Chinese government and Chinese reporters. Meggyesy then stood up and said that he could represent the foreign reporters in offering a word, that Japan cannot evade blame for the Manchurian Incident, and that justice will surely prevail in the future. Meggyesy also made an analogy, which drew applause from the audience. Finally, Nie Shifen, the director of the Journalism Department of Yenching University, gave a speech in which he highly praised China's current non-resistance and calm attitude, and said that the Chinese should not deal with the Japanese with military actions. If the Chinese can continue this attitude for six months, there would be a significant impact on its economy and commerce. Xie Fusheng gave the closing remarks, and the meeting adjourned.

National Government Disaster Relief Committee

Contract for Purchasing American Wheat 108

Announced by Chairman Song Yesterday

Song Ziwen, Chairman of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, announced at 4:00 PM yesterday the National Government's contract with the U.S. Department of Agriculture for purchasing American wheat. The full text is as follows:

(1) The U.S. Grain Market Price Stabilization Committee, with the approval of the Department of Agriculture, is willing to sell 450,000 short tons (2,000 lbs.) of U.S. wheat (No. 2 Western White Wheat) to the National Government of the Republic of China. The National Government is willing to purchase this wheat. The cost of shipping the wheat to the Pacific ports of the United States for loading shall be borne by the United States. (2) The seller has the right to substitute flour for the wheat, but the amount of flour shall not exceed half of the total amount. The price of flour shall be determined by comparison. (3) The Pacific ports of the United States from which the American wheat is shipped shall be selected by the seller. The quantity of wheat shipped each time is as follows: 90,000 tons for the end of September and the entire month of October; 75,000 tons each month for November, December, January, and February; and 60,000 tons for March. The date of shipment each month shall be determined by the buyer, but the seller must be notified five days in advance. (4) The price of wheat each time shall be based on the market price on the date the bill of lading is issued at the port of shipment. (5) Each time the buyer receives the American wheat and/or flour, it shall prepare a purchase receipt for the wheat by the National Government and deliver it to the representative designated by the seller. The date on the receipt shall be the same as the date on the bill of lading. The principal and interest of the aforementioned debt shall be paid in U.S. dollars in New York. The interest on the wheat shall be calculated at 4% per annum, payable on June 30 and December 31 of each year. The wheat shall be repaid in three installments, with one-third payable each time. The first installment shall be paid on December 31, 1934 (Year 23 of the Republic of China), the second installment on December 31, 1935, and the third installment on December 31, 1936. (6) When the buyer receives a batch of American wheat, it shall appoint a representative to deliver a signed temporary receipt to the seller as proof. This temporary receipt shall be combined into three copies of a definitive total receipt in accordance with Article 5 within a short period of time. (7) The aforementioned wheat and/or flour shall be used exclusively for charitable relief in the flood-stricken areas of China. (8) American merchant ships shall be given priority for shipping the American wheat and/or flour. However, if ships from other countries are berthed at the port of shipment during the time of shipment and are able to load the wheat under the conditions stipulated in Article 3 and their freight is lower than that of American ships, the buyer shall have the right to hire those ships instead.

Xu Shiying and Zhu Qinglan 110

Request the Dispatch of Personnel to Supervise Relief Distribution

Xu Shiying and Zhu Ziqiao submitted a request to the National Government through the Urgent Relief Committee, requesting that supervisory committee members be dispatched to various disaster-stricken provinces to earnestly investigate relief distribution personnel. They stated that the extent of the disaster areas, the severity of the disaster situation, and the number of disaster victims in the various provinces this year were unprecedented in a century. The government is deeply concerned and has allocated funds for relief. Qinglan has been entrusted with the task of disaster relief work, and he bears a heavy responsibility. He will do his best to act with conscience and integrity and has hired relief commissioners to various provinces, all of whom he trusts. However, the personnel dispatched by the commissioners to investigate and distribute relief funds, distribute relief goods, and those used in future labor relief and agricultural relief projects are numerous. Qinglan's ears and eyes are limited, and the relief funds are of utmost importance, even the smallest amount. If there is any negligence, it would not only be a matter of conscience but also be intolerable to public opinion. Thinking of this, he feels apprehensive. Furthermore, Xu Shiying previously received two million yuan in salt tax treasury bonds allocated by the Central Government, which were mortgaged for one million yuan in cash. The Executive Yuan ordered the various members of the Relief Committee to carry the funds to Hubei, Hunan, Anhui, Henan, Jiangxi, Jiangsu, and Zhejiang provinces for urgent relief. This matter is also of great importance and should be subject to strict investigation. Qinglan and Shiying propose that the committee submit a request to the National Government to order the Supervisory Yuan to dispatch supervisory committee members to various disaster-stricken provinces to conduct thorough investigations into all aspects of urgent relief, labor relief, and agricultural relief. Any embezzlement or misappropriation of relief funds, as well as fraudulent relief distribution, collusion with local authorities to fraudulently claim relief, and other fraudulent activities related to relief work, should be severely punished according to the law upon verification. However, those who undertake relief work with integrity and have made significant contributions should also be rewarded by the government to encourage others.

Dangtu's Losses Reach Ten Million Yuan 111

The Dangtu Red Swastika Society's on-site report on the water disaster states that the county has a total of over 750,000 mu of land, of which over 678,000 mu of farmland were submerged by floods, and over 70,000 mu of farmland were subsequently damaged by wind. The total population of the county is over 350,000, of which over 320,000 are disaster victims. The farmland in various townships was submerged by floods, and the few mountain fields were also damaged by wind, resulting in a harvest of less than 10%. The disaster caused the deaths of 1,617 males and 1,309 females. 45,955 houses collapsed, totaling 137,865 rooms. 2,078 heads of livestock were swept away, valued at 83,120 yuan. The total losses for the county are estimated to be over 8.87 million yuan.

Hubei Relief Office Expedites Production of Epidemic Prevention Oil 112

The Hubei Water Disaster Urgent Relief Committee's office in Shanghai received a telegram yesterday from Chairman He Chengjun of the Wuhan branch, which stated, "The emergency epidemic prevention oil previously transported here has been very effective, especially for children suffering from epidemics, who recover after taking it once. Although 300,000 bottles have been transported before and after, the disaster area is too large and the supply is insufficient. We urgently request that you raise funds to purchase 200,000 bottles, no matter what, and expedite the process to transport them to Hubei as soon as possible to save the disaster victims." It is reported that after receiving the telegram, the office is currently negotiating with the pharmacist Mr. Fu Nianci to work day and night to expedite production, aiming to transport it to Wuhan within two weeks. The severity of the disaster in Hubei Province this year is truly unprecedented. The number of bottles of medicine for treating epidemics alone has been distributed to hundreds of thousands, which is still not enough, which shows the severity of the epidemic.

Korean Residents Held a General Meeting Yesterday 115

Six Resolutions Passed

Since Japan forcibly occupied the Eastern Provinces, various circles of Korean residents in Shanghai have repeatedly expressed their deep sorrow. At 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, Korean residents held another general meeting on Minguo Road. Regular Resumption of Hankou-Yichang Air Route 116

September 29

The China National Aviation Corporation's mail transport plane between Hankou and Yichang was temporarily suspended due to the sudden rise of floodwaters in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River and the excessive current, which prevented the plane from landing. Now, reports have been received from stations along the river that the floodwaters have receded and the plane landing docks have been properly repaired. It has been decided that the Hankou-Yichang line will resume service on September 29 (Tuesday). The flight times and schedules will remain the same, and passengers and mail will be carried as usual. It will be possible to travel from Shanghai to Yichang in one day.

Record of the Third Annual Meeting of the Child Welfare Association 117

Starting with Children's Education

Washing Away China's Humiliation

The China Child Welfare Association held its third annual meeting yesterday at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. More than 20 people attended, including Chairman Kong Xiangxi, Vice-Chairman Luo Yunyan, Mrs. Guo Bingwen, Hu Yigu, Zhang Zhijiang (represented by Weng Guoxun), Zheng Hongnian (represented by Tang Tonghou), Wang Xiaozai, and Zhu Shaoping. Chairman Kong Yongzhi gave a speech, saying that the Child Welfare Association was holding its third annual meeting amidst the solemn and enthusiastic anti-Japanese movement, and that he felt that this had a very profound meaning worth pondering carefully. He said that this time Japan had inflicted great insult on China, but China could not directly stop it and implement normal defense, but had to beg for pity from the League of Nations and other countries, which was heartbreaking. He recalled that in the early 19th century, Prussia was often ravaged by France, so the people of the country prepared for revenge. Iron Chancellor Bismarck first educated the people and rectified primary school education in the country. Sure enough, in the battle of Shi Dan in 1870, the French Emperor Napoleon III was captured and a great victory was won, washing away the humiliation of the past. He felt that this matter could be used as a reference for us. If we want to save the country from the root and wash away today's humiliation, we must start with children's education. However, it is shameful to say that Chinese children do not receive adequate education, nor do they receive adequate care. Since care cannot even be talked about, how can we talk about education? Just look at the countless children who died in this water disaster. Others, in ordinary times, are poorly clothed and fed, beg on the streets, and suffer from diseases due to lack of hygiene. What can we do to remedy this? Children are the future masters of the country. Now that the future masters of our country are not adequately cared for and educated, how can our country become strong? Since it cannot become strong, how can it wash away national humiliation? The Child Welfare Association is a Chinese people's organization whose greatest purpose is to seek happiness for Chinese children, in other words, to cultivate China's vitality and lay the foundation for China. From now on, we hope that it can awaken the awareness of the people of the country, first solve the basic problem of providing for children, and then solve the problem of educating children, not only enabling children throughout the country to receive adequate care, but also enabling them to receive adequate education. Then, the strength of our China will only be a matter of time, and all national humiliations can be washed away. Next, the officials were elected: Chairman Kong Yongzhi, Chief Vice-Chairman Luo Yunyan, Second Vice-Chairman Mrs. Liu Zhanen, Accountant Gao Fengchi, Deputy Accountant Li Daonan, Secretary Chen Heqin. The following were elected to the committee: Fu Kuangzhuo, Mrs. Fu Bulaun, Hu Yigu, Mrs. Guo Bingwen, Niu Huisheng, Le Lingsheng, Ms. Ding Juejing, Hu Xuanming, Fei Meisheng, Pan Gongzhan, Hai Muhua, Lai Sili, Jiang Changchuan. Temporary motions: (1) Send a telegram to all compatriots, asking them to be determined to die for the country (motion drafted by Chen Zhengfan), (2) Send a telegram to the National Government, asking it to implement proper defense, (3) Send a telegram to the Japanese Women's Association, asking it to urge its government to reflect, and to the American Child Welfare Association, asking it to uphold justice. Another telegram was sent nationwide, stating, "All compatriots across the country, as transferred by the Shanghai newspapers, are hereby informed that this time the violent Japanese invaded our borders and massacred our people, and the most brutal thing is that innocent children were also harmed. If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? If we do not resist this, how can we establish a nation? At this time of great difficulty, all of our people should be determined to die for the country, our government leaders should work together in harmony, and our country's future children's education should pay more attention to cultivating national strength in order to lay the foundation for the country and resist foreign aggression. Urgent words, hoping for joint efforts. The China Child Welfare Association Third Annual Meeting Koutou."

Ministry of Industry

Explanation of the Reason for Inspecting Tea Leaves 119

A telegram from business representatives of foreign tea firms to the Ministry of Industry states: "To Zheng Ziyu and others, representatives of foreign tea firms from Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Shanghai. We have received your telegrams. Tea has always been a special product of our country, sold worldwide. Tea from Japan, India, Ceylon, and other places emerged later, but they have been able to research and improve, and European and American markets have been seized. Chinese tea adheres to old ways, and is often adulterated with coloring, leading to a daily decline in sales. In the first year of the Republic of China, exports were more than 1.4 million dan. Since then, they have declined year by year, even to more than 400,000 dan. Although the years 1928 and 1929 saw an increase to more than 900,000 dan, the latest customs records show that exports in 1930 fell again to just over 690,000 dan. In recent years, Chinese tea has relied on Russia as a market of last resort, while Japanese green tea sales to Russia have increased year by year since 1926, exceeding Chinese tea exports last year. Chinese tea is failing step by step. If we do not catch up quickly, what will the future hold? The government is conducting inspections to increase the international trade reputation, promote improvements in tea production, and issued instructions to the Construction Departments of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi provinces in April of this year to urge tea merchants in tea-producing counties and cities to improve manufacturing and refrain from coloring and adulteration, in order to save the industry. Your telegrams state that tea merchants are striving to improve the quality of their products, and that the people's efforts reflect the government's concerns. Have there been any improvements in fact? Colored tea has been rejected by the American market. Although a portion of the population in other countries still needs it due to habit and is temporarily allowed for export, the actual fact is that using Berlin Blue and similar pigments for coloring, when ingested, will produce highly toxic hydrocyanic acid gas upon encountering acidic stomach fluids, causing severe damage to health. Inspection at the place of origin is essential, and the Ministry is planning this carefully. However, export inspection is international in nature. In order to prevent fraud by Chinese and foreign tea merchants during the process, it cannot be abolished. Article 2 of the Tea Inspection Regulations stipulates that applications for inspection should be made to the local commodity inspection bureau or its branches, referring to the inspection bureaus or their branches in tea export ports. The telegrams’ reference to inspection at the place of origin is a misunderstanding. As for the representatives' concern about whether the inspectors' judgments are fair and impartial, if such a situation exists, tea merchants can request re-inspection according to the regulations or make a practical report. How can speculative matters be used as reasons for opposition? Furthermore, the telegrams state that foreign merchants are watching and prices are falling sharply upon hearing of the crackdown. Although tea prices fluctuated in mid-July, this was a temporary market phenomenon. How can this be used as an excuse for inspection? Since July 23, sales have been brisk. In early August, the tea market was even more prosperous. High-quality green teas such as Zhen Mei were exceptionally strong, rising to more than ten taels. All newspapers can verify this. What is the explanation? It should be known that the government has shown great care in exempting tea from export taxes, but this still cannot reverse the decline. The key lies in the poor quality of tea production. It is conceivable that inspecting tea is a policy already set by the government. Japan, Taiwan, Java, Ceylon, and other places have precedents. The main purpose is to directly stop the coloring and adulteration of tea, and indirectly promote the improvement and manufacturing of tea, in order to strengthen consumers' faith and compete in the international market. The representatives do not understand the trend of overseas trade in recent years, and their telegrams opposing and obstructing the overall plan are inappropriate. The request to stop the inspection is difficult to approve. If the representatives believe that there is room for improvement in the inspection procedures, they can submit their opinions for consideration." Ministry of Industry, Seal.

Response to Zhu Ziqiao's Telegram 120

General Zhu Ziqiao sent a telegram requesting all parties to cease conflict and resist foreign aggression. Military, political, business, and civilians across the country unanimously supported it. The following are the replies received yesterday:

Liang Guanying's Telegram: Urgent. To Mr. Zhu Ziqiao of the Shanghai National Disaster Relief Committee. I have received your telegram. Your pain over the Japanese寇's aggression and your presentation of the principles for national salvation are inspiring. Anyone with patriotism should be awakened. Guanying is a soldier and is publicly serving the country. I am inspired to work harder. I humbly express my sincerity. Please understand. Liang Guanying, Seal.

Shaoxing Telegram: To Mr. Zhu Ziqiao of the Yunnan Road Fundraising Committee for Urgent Disaster Relief in various provinces. The people of Shaoxing admire your integrity. Upon hearing of your efforts in disaster relief, we do not hesitate to contribute our meager efforts to help. Reading your telegram, your words are truly piercing. It will surely move the world. As citizens of this country, we should follow your lead. We wish you success and urge you to take care of yourself. The Shaoxing Fundraising Committee for Urgent Disaster Relief in various provinces, Seal.

Three Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad 121

The three bandits smile calmly

Loudly request immediate execution

The kidnappers, Lu A'gen from Yangzhou, 32 years old; Wu Shenxian, a local, 35 years old; and Wang Songlin from Pudong, 26 years old, were arrested for kidnapping Chen Tufan, the owner of a construction factory, on December 19th last year at 9:35 PM on Pingwang Street, and Li Weiqing, who ran a real estate business, on Guangxi Road at 1:00 AM on February 8th this year, demanding huge ransoms. After the cases were investigated, they were arrested by the Lao Zha and Hongkou police stations and handed over to the First Special District Court. They were sentenced to death. The sentences were submitted to the higher authorities for approval. Yesterday morning, the execution date arrived. The police took Lu A'gen and the other two from the West Prison and brought them to the Third Criminal Court. At around 9:00 AM, Judge Cheng Shangfeng took his seat and asked Lu and the others if they had any last words. He also notified their families. According to Wu Shenxian, the main culprit was actually Liang Chengyu. He had been told not to incriminate him during the previous interrogation. He now asked the court to allow his father, Wu Zhangzhang, to take custody of all his tools and equipment, as well as his wife's jewelry, rings, and other items, at Liang Dongsheng's fruit store on the second floor of the 16th Pier. He also requested that his father collect his body. Wang Songlin requested that the court send a letter to Wang Shuji at No. 12 Huayuan Lane, North Zhejiang Road, to be forwarded to his family in Pudong, informing them that the execution had been carried out and that he had nothing else to say. Lu A'gen stated that Liang Chengyu was the main culprit in the kidnapping of both Chen and Li. Previously, during the appeal period, he offered them 10,000 yuan for their future expenses, but they refused because they were about to be executed and had no use for the money. He also requested that a message be sent to his father at No. 12 Leyu Lane, Wuzhen Road, asking him to collect his body. All three defendants smiled calmly and showed no fear of death. Judge Cheng ordered the Chinese and foreign police to take them away and escort them onto a car, along with the case files and photographs, and drive them to the Caohejing Second Prison execution ground. The Local Court appointed Prosecutor Shen Taoming as the execution officer. He then ordered Police Chief Xu Jinqing and Police Inspector Chen Xihui to supervise the executioners, Gu Hanqing, Yin Daoxu, Xu Guoguang, Lu Conghe, Zhou Qiwen, Zhu Wanyuan, Xiong Dingcheng, Liu Fu, and Zhao Mingyuan, who traveled in cars to the execution ground. After the judge and Warden Dong Changmin took their seats, the three prisoners were brought in for questioning. After the questioning, all three loudly requested immediate execution and asked for a clean job. The judge ordered the executioners to take them away and execute them by firing squad. The bodies were inspected by Inspector Shen. He then ordered the hall to collect and seal the bodies for burial.

Arrest of Two or Three Russian Bandits Planning to Kidnap Sofa 122

The North China Times reports that the Public Concession police have arrested five Russians in the past 24 hours. After seizing three handguns, some bullets, and criminal documents, they uncovered a major plot to kidnap the wealthy Jewish businessman, Sofa. It is reported that the police had heard about the plot earlier and assigned two Russian detectives to investigate. After more than two months of investigation, they finally tracked down a Russian man in the French Concession on Thursday night and arrested him. Four hours later, they arrested another Russian youth in the French Concession. Subsequently, they searched the youth's residence and found several criminal documents clearly stating the plan to kidnap Sofa. The next morning, they escorted the two men to the Special District Court. After questioning, they were detained pending further investigation. A few hours before the two men were brought to the court, three more people were arrested in the French Concession. One of them confessed to having rented a hideout for the kidnap victims. When they searched the place, it was empty. They found only two handguns, two dozen bullets, and two hemp ropes with blackened paper pasted on the inside of the glasses. Two hours later, they found another handgun and some bullets at another location in the French Concession. It is reported that they had planned to kidnap Sofa last Sunday, but the plan was aborted for some reason.

International Radio Station is Busy 123

Due to the serious Sino-Japanese negotiations in recent days, the International Radio Station, which is dedicated to being the voice of China, is extremely busy. The U.S.-China route has doubled in business. Due to poor water cable direct lines, merchants sending messages to various merchants via the Atlantic water line have switched to the International Radio Station. Its accuracy and speed are far superior to that water line.

Leprosy Society

Assisting in the Construction of the Qiongan Leprosy Hospital 124

The China Leprosy Relief Association recently received official letters from the Haikou Chamber of Commerce and the Qiongshan County Magistrate on Hainan Island, Guangdong, requesting the association to subsidize the construction of the Qiongya Leprosy Hospital. A meeting of the executive directors was convened yesterday, attended by Madam Xiao Zhiji, Li Yuanxin, Li Guansen, Zhu Shaoping, Wu Zhijian, and others. First, Mr. Shi Dingye, representative of the Qiongan Leprosy Hospital Preparatory Committee, reported, "There are about 500 lepers on Hainan Island. The local government has always ignored them and has no thorough relief measures, which has a profound impact on the nation's health. Concerned individuals have organized the Qiongya Leprosy Hospital Preparatory Committee. They have already raised 5,000 yuan. The county government plans to allocate more than 30 mu of barren government land as a base. There are also bricks and stones from the demolition of the old city that can be allocated as building materials. However, according to the budget, the funds are still huge. We hope that your association can provide assistance." It was decided to provide a subsidy of 5,000 yuan so that it can be completed as soon as possible.

Wusong Water Police

Large-Scale Suppression of Sea Bandits 125

In recent days, sea bandits outside the port of Wusong have been gathering more and more, looting everywhere. It was learned from the fourth district of the Wusong Water Police that the bandits were gathered at Daan Port, the border between Tongzhou and Haimen counties, with hundreds of people fully armed. They were all on sailing ships and in shallow waters, making it difficult to suppress them. It is now known that District Chief Jiang personally set off on the Junhe cruiser yesterday morning to supervise the teams, surround, and suppress the bandits. He ordered Team Leader Gong Mianqin of the 17th Team to lead the Pingyang Zhenyu, two warships, and patrol boats from Hupu. The Jinghai and Jingdong warships set off from Haimen. He also ordered Team Leader Xie Zezhi of the 18th Team to lead his team on a warship from Xiaoyang Port in Nantong. The 16th Team remained in Hupu to block the bandits. He also sent a telegram to the Haimen County Police to intercept the bandits along the coast in the ports of Niuhong, Daan, and Laohong. He also ordered all fleets to meet at Songji Port at 5:00 PM this afternoon to receive orders for the second phase of the search plan in order to thoroughly eliminate the bandits.

Rickshaw Puller

Embezzling Money Left Behind by Passengers 126

The car owner found out and reported it to the police

Waiting for the owner to come and claim it

Rickshaw puller Hu Rongfa drove his rickshaw to Moore Road the other day. A woman hired him to go to the train station and left a yellow wallet on the car when she got off. Hu brought it back and opened it. There were 130 yuan in banknotes inside. Hu was overjoyed at this windfall and told everyone about it. His colleagues Ma Rongde, Xu Chunhe, Chen Chunyu, and Zhou Fengbao found out about it and asked him to share the money. Rickshaw owner Xue Zhengfa found out about it. According to the police regulations, the car owner is responsible for any items lost by passengers in the car, so he secretly reported it to the police. The police arrested Hu Rongfa and the four people who intended to share the money and detained them in the police station. Yesterday, they were taken to the criminal court of the Second Special Court. Police lawyer Chen Ming explained the case, stating that the first defendant had committed the crime of misappropriating lost property under Article 358 of the Criminal Law and requested that he be prosecuted. Then, car owner Xue Zhengfa reported the previous situation. Hu Rongfa confessed that the wallet was left on the car by a woman who was in a hurry to catch the train and that he did not steal it intentionally. Ma and the other four confessed that they had borrowed money from Hu and did not dare to share it. The judge ordered Hu Rongfa to be remanded in custody and to wait for the owner to come to court for further questioning. Ma and the other four were released on bail pending further investigation.

An Old Woman Deceives a Young Woman to Come to Shanghai 127

On the pretext of introducing her as a maid

Intending to sell her into prostitution

Qin Li, a young woman from Xiangshan, Ningbo, is 26 years old. Because her family was poor, she worked as a maid in Ningbo City and earned only three yuan a month. An old woman, Zhang Feng, persuaded her to go to Shanghai to work as a maid, saying that she could earn six yuan a month. Since the young woman had no one to introduce her, the old woman took advantage of her weakness and desire for money, pretended to be benevolent, and offered to introduce her. She brought the young woman to Shanghai and took her to her daughter's house in Cangqiao Head, Xiaonanmen. A few days ago, she went to the Meifeng brothel to sell her, saying that she had a daughter-in-law who was willing to become a prostitute. The brothel sent someone to the old woman's house to see the young woman and asked her about her background and told her about the prostitution. The young woman cried and hit her head against the pillar. The people in the brothel fled. At that time, a patrol officer arrived and asked about the situation. The old woman was detained in the first district and the first office. Yesterday, she was transferred to the court for interrogation.

A Child Dies After Being Knocked Down in a Fight 128

Waiting to see the prescription for further verification

A three-month-old baby, A'niu, son of Tang Heshang, a Ningbo native residing at No. 919 Dongyouheng Road, was sleeping on a small wooden bed on the afternoon of the 14th of this month at about 1:00 PM. It was unexpected that Zhang A'qing and his wife, Kong, also Ningbo natives living in the same residence, had a quarrel and fought each other. As Mrs. Zhang fell, she accidentally knocked over the wooden bed, and A'niu fell to the ground, was injured, and became ill. He died on the afternoon of the 24th at 6:00 PM. The body was sent to the Fei Lun Road Morgue. Prosecutor Guo of the First Special Court went to the morgue and determined that the child died from a fall. Therefore, the child's father sued the Huishan Police Station, which sent Detective Huang Fugen to arrest Zhang A'qing and his wife, Zhang Kong, and detain them separately. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu stated the case. Then, the plaintiff, Tang Heshang, reported the situation and said that the child, A'niu, had stopped eating milk after being knocked down by the defendants and that seeing a doctor had been ineffective. However, the prescription had not been brought today. A neighbor surnamed Wang witnessed the incident. When asked, the two defendants denied knocking over A'niu's bed during the fight, claiming that the child died of illness. After reviewing the confession, Judge Shen Bingrong ordered the two defendants to be remanded in custody separately and to be summoned for further questioning at a later date. He also ordered Tang Heshang to bring the prescription to the next hearing.

Xiao Zhiming Commits Suicide in a Hotel 129

Xiao Zhiming, a 21-year-old Suzhou native who claimed to be a southern goods merchant, checked into room number six of the Wankang Inn, a small inn opened by Wu Wanli, a Ningbo native, at No. 115 Lixian Lane, Dongzilaishui Street, French Concession, on the evening of the 20th of this month. For some unknown reason, he suddenly had suicidal thoughts and swallowed raw opium. After the waiter found out, he was immediately sent to Renji Hospital. However, he was deeply poisoned and died at 6:00 AM yesterday despite the rescue efforts. The hospital reported the death to the police, who carried the body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch of the morgue. It was impossible to investigate the deceased's family. The report was made by Prosecutor Lou Guanguang of the Second Special Court, who determined that the deceased had committed suicide by taking poison and ordered that the body be collected by Tongren Fuyuan Hall. After the inspection, the police took a photo of the body. Later, the hall prepared a coffin and transported it to the Pudong cemetery for burial, waiting for relatives to claim it.

Huang Xiuming's Divorce Conditions 130

800 Yuan Alimony

Huang Xiuming hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Civil Mediation Court of the Second Special Court, stating that the petitioner had previously married Yan Hansan, who lived on Laoshifu Road. After the marriage, she was often abused, and her husband was addicted to opium, requiring the petitioner to serve him all night. If she did not comply, she would be humiliated. Therefore, the petitioner requested mediation because she felt that there was no happiness in her future. She requested that the divorce be granted and that she be awarded 3,000 yuan in alimony. Yesterday, both parties were summoned to court for mediation. First, the petitioner recounted the previous situation. The defendant did not appear, but his lawyer represented him, stating that the petitioner's claims were inconsistent with the facts. The petitioner was only a concubine and was treated very well after the marriage and there was no abuse. However, because they were a modest family, there was frugality. The defendant was an accountant at the Nanshi Water Plant and earned more than 30 yuan a month. The defendant did not object to the petitioner's request for a divorce, but the amount of alimony requested by the petitioner was too large and could be reduced to 200 or 300 yuan. The petitioner's lawyer stated that it would take at least 1,500 yuan to reach a settlement. After repeated persuasion by the judge, the two parties compromised on 800 yuan. Both parties agreed, and each of their lawyers signed the record. The mediation was then declared successful.

Haiping Ship Wrecks Two Cargo Ships 131

Yesterday, Chen Yinsheng and other lightermen were carrying two ships of sorghum, a total of 402 bags, for a certain company to another port. Unexpectedly, at about 1:00 PM, the two ships were outside the China Merchants Bureau pier when the Haiping ship turned around, creating waves. The two ships were unable to avoid them and were wrecked. Everyone on board went into the water. Fortunately, the water patrol team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, led by police chief Fu Jixiang, was patrolling the river and saw the situation. They immediately tried to rescue them and rescued several people who had fallen into the water. However, all the goods on the two ships have sunk to the bottom of the river, resulting in considerable losses.

Giving away Guohuo Sheng Dan at the venue

This city's Xie Xing Pharmaceutical Factory is one of our country's leading pharmaceutical industries, issuing Bailinji, Bu Lida, Jiufu Milk White Cod Liver Oil, etc., all of which have won deep social welcome with the latest scientific preparations. Its seasonal health products Sheng Dan is a kind of acupuncture industry that competes with Japanese Rendan, with low prices and even exceeding its efficacy, which is enough to be a representative product for resisting Japanese medicines. At this time when the people all know how to promote Guohuo, sales are extremely smooth, and since the violent Japanese invasion of the Northeast, the boycott of Japanese goods has intensified, and seasonal health products, especially Sheng Dan, are in demand. Therefore, the factory is working hard to speed up production in order to do its best in the anti-Japanese and national salvation work. Yesterday, the entire staff of the anti-Japanese and national salvation citizens' assembly at the Public Sports Ground in this city, from managers to factory directors, participated unanimously. Each held slogan flags, with black cloths wrapped around their arms, showing great enthusiasm, and prepared a number of Sheng Dan samples, which were distributed on the spot, so that the patriotic people who participated in the meeting could taste this Guohuo Sheng Dan. It is said that Sheng Dan can be obtained to give birth, and the country's vitality, or the great omen in this tone seems humorous, but according to the duties of the industrial and commercial circles, it is possible to do their best to create alternative products to introduce to the Chinese people, leak the crevices as much as possible, and restore the rights and interests, and it is also almost a way to save the country.

Mr. Li Mincui asked (which is more important, saving the country or filial piety)

In this critical period of national survival, as citizens, of course, everyone should unite and think about countermeasures. Recently, the Anti-Japanese Association organized a volunteer group, which is also a powerful countermeasure. I am a shop assistant in a small country. I have some understanding of the idea of saving the country, so I want to join the group and serve the country. However, when I think about the family relationship, I cannot give it up, because I have no father since I was a child, and I only rely on my loving mother to endure all kinds of hardships to raise me up. Now her hope is to see me have a good family and career, and want to have a grandson. If I now, because of the impulse of patriotism, turn my back on my family and join the army, then I will definitely resent and cry bitterly. Now it is the time of my old age, or there may be unexpected events, then my national salvation ambition has not succeeded, and the crime of unfilial piety has been spread to the local party, so I want to ask you gentlemen to think of an appropriate way to solve this important matter,

(Cause) Your one thought of loving the country and one thought of not forgetting filial piety is respectable. At this time, because of Japan's atrocities, volunteer groups are organized everywhere, the purpose is to exercise the body, do military exercises, and establish the foundation of national self-improvement, and it is not to go to ambushes immediately. It is too far away from fighting. Since you have this good intention, you should tell your mother earnestly and clearly how unreasonable the Japanese are this time, how terrible the future of China is, what the national obligations should be, and how if we do not join forces to save ourselves, we will all perish. I think my mother will not object. Also tell my mother about the purpose of organizing the volunteer group, and at this time I can't talk about the situation of fighting, my mother will naturally be more at ease. Didn't you see in the third edition of this newspaper yesterday that the Zhejiang Provincial Government's military training of the old and the weak are all being trained?

News from a Man of Wufeng Mountain 137

(Deliberations on the People's Food Problem, Production Problem, and Commercial Studies Books in Wuyuan)

My Wuyuan has many mountains and little land. Besides growing tea and trees, the people have no other means of livelihood. Therefore, most of them do business abroad. In recent years, there have been natural and man-made disasters, and the commercial situation is sluggish. Many businessmen are uneasy in their businesses. Moreover, the hometown is often disturbed by Jiangxi bandits. Rice is as expensive as pearls, and firewood is as expensive as cassia. Most of the grain relies on relief from Jiangxi. In recent years, the communists in that province have been rampant, and local gentry have prohibited the transportation of rice out of the province, leaving the people of Wuyuan waiting to die. Please instruct me on the following: 1. Since Wuyuan has little land, what kind of practical industries should the people engage in to make a living? Please instruct me on the following: 2. Because I am troubled by economic difficulties, I cannot enter a commercial school. What kind of books should I study on my own to learn about commerce? Please instruct me on the following: 3. Please answer the above three questions in the newspaper.

(Reply) 1. Most of the food for the people of Wuyuan is transported from Xiuning, Jiangxi, and other places for relief. Now, due to the rampancy of the communists in Jiangxi, the people are fleeing, the rice production has decreased, and exports are prohibited. Xiuning is also unable to help due to this year's poor harvest. Natural and man-made disasters have followed one after another, causing great difficulties. The food problem of the people of Wuyuan is indeed a very important and difficult problem. Concrete solutions are difficult to answer in a hurry.

2. Since Wuyuan has little land, the people's production can only start from the family. Such as raising chickens, raising pigs, spinning yarn, weaving cloth, and sewing, etc., are all easy to do. In addition to the original experience of raising chickens and pigs, it is best to add new methods and improve and study them. This would be even better. (The Commercial Press has published the latest "Pig Raising Method," and the Jiangwan Chinese Chicken Farm has published the "Chinese Chicken Raising Technique," both of which can be consulted.)

3. Since you are studying in a shop and want to study commerce in your spare time, this is a very good idea. The Commercial Press has published "Retail Studies," which costs 50 cents. You can buy one to read first. It is best to be attentive in your service, apply what you have learned from books to practice, and accumulate experience over time. You can gain a wealth of experience. What do you think?

To resist Japan and save the country, everyone should work hard from their own position. This is really the most important and most effective thing. Then our press should do two things:

World Small News Record 143

Chaplin Initiates Basket Balancing Competition The screen's comical king Chaplin has become a global figure. Be it a land of culture or a land of barbarity, almost no one does not know Chaplin. He has received a warm welcome in various countries upon returning to Europe. After arriving in his birthplace of England, the entire nation has gone mad with joy in welcoming him. He had a whimsical idea in London, suddenly initiating a competition of balancing baskets on the head, scheduled to be held on the 10th of this month. For anyone who gets champagne, Chaplin will award them twenty pounds sterling. At one point, approximately forty individuals signed up to join. In the middle of August, many people were already practicing in the streets of London, walking around with a large stack of baskets balanced on their heads. Each person had a trainer, accompanied by several sponsors who would watch their movements and correct their posture at any moment. According to the rules of the competition stipulated by Chaplin, each person must stack twelve baskets, each weighing half a bushel, on their head and race for a quarter of a mile. The first to arrive will get champagne. According to general consensus, Mr. W. Sparks from Boroogh Market

To Save the Country, We Must Rely on Our Own Strength 144

— Wu Yu

Is most promising. And Boroogh Market happens to be where Chaplin spent his childhood fishing. However, it is said that there are also several strong contenders from Covent Garden who can compete with him. Now that September 10th has passed, it is unknown who has won.

Evil neighbors are using their violent military force to wreak havoc on our Chinese people. The tragedy of Wanbaoshan has not yet ended, and the storm of the Nakamura Incident has risen again. Recently, they have even disregarded humanity and violated public reason, brazenly invading our Shenyang and encroaching on our hinterland. Alas, our China, having survived disaster, faces death and destruction every day. As news of the alarm spreads, anyone with a bit of spirit is bound to have their eyes tear and hair stand on end, filled with grief and indignation. However, the five-minute enthusiasm of the people has been tried again and again, and the techniques of resistance are nothing more than holding meetings, sending telegrams, shouting slogans, and posting slogans. Even those who go further are nothing more than petitioning the central government to rectify officialdom and prepare for negotiations, etc. All are empty words and of no practical use. Just look at the newspapers in the past two days, which are full of such empty discussions, playing the old trick of armchair strategizing. Alas, when disaster is imminent, is there still room for you to wield your pens and play with ink, using this to show off your telegrams? I believe that all paper work is useless. We must start with the most basic, most effective, and most concrete methods. I believe that appealing to the League of Nations and issuing declarations are both dispensable. The first step must be to do our best to fulfill our responsibility to save the country, bit by bit. Although the effect of one person is limited, the power of the entire nation is considerable. Although it may sound like old news, it is better than just spouting empty words. We should do everything we can. I will list them below.

(1) Swear to never buy Japanese goods, from the individual to the family, to the village, and to the whole country.

(2) Do our best to donate money to save the country, and send it to the most reliable bank to be used to purchase airplanes, warships, weapons, ammunition, and food. (3) Each village and neighborhood should organize its own volunteer team, with ten people as a small group and one hundred people as a large group, providing their own rations, weapons, and ammunition. Then, elect someone with military knowledge to be the commander to prepare for advancing, fighting, retreating, and defending. Relying solely on the power of the special government is not enough.

(4) Organize a people's salvation group to gather the armed forces of the people as a backing for the government.

What has been said above still requires everyone to be united and of one mind to be effective. However, it is better to seek help from oneself than from others. We can only save ourselves, then we can save others, and then we can save the country. Otherwise, it will only be a flurry of busy paper telegrams, which will only be laughed at by the wooden clogs of the eastern neighbors.

The Need for National Shame Advertisements 145

— Geng Sheng

There are many anti-Japanese propaganda items posted in the city. However, they all require people who have received several years of education and know a few words to fully understand them. Isn't it true that there are more people who have not received education in our China? Not to mention the slogans posted on the trams, which pass by in an instant and cannot be seen clearly, most of the various slogans posted on the walls are also incomprehensible. Moreover, they will disappear in the event of violent winds and heavy rain. Therefore, pictures are important.

Aren't there many empty advertising boards towering in the streets? Why not paint a few eye-catching, simple, and obvious national shame advertisements on them using high-quality oil paint? They will permanently watch the passersby, making them aware that China's national enemy is Japan. In their shallow minds, they should not forget it. (Tyrannical Japan)

The walls outside schools can also be painted with a few national shame paintings so that the future masters of China who go to school every day will have our national shame deeply imprinted in their minds.

Please use coercive means on foreign cloth stores, southern goods stores, paper stores, toy stores, etc. (I am afraid that it is not necessary because their shopkeepers are also Chinese and have hearts and are not deaf and blind.) Paint a few of these eye-catching things on the front of their counters so that people who buy things will be spared from indirectly giving their hard-earned money to the enemy after seeing these eye-catching things. On the city standard clock that is under construction, its base and the bottom of the clock face can also be painted with a few pictures. In short, paint a few pictures wherever it is possible so that the people's hearts and minds are constantly alerted, so that they can reach the point of directly attacking Huanglong and avenging the national shame in the future.
